					Rosamunde, D.797 (Schubert, Franz)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>10 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1823
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Incidental_music&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Incidental music</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voice%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voice, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="34 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voices_and_chorus_with_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voices and chorus with orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Rosamunde, Fürstin von Zypern
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Schubert,_Franz" title="Category:Schubert, Franz">Schubert, Franz</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>D.797
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IFS 621
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>10 movements (Overture + 9):
<dl><dd>Overture
<dl><dd>a. from <i><a href="/wiki/Alfonso_und_Estrella,_D.732_(Schubert,_Franz)" title="Alfonso und Estrella, D.732 (Schubert, Franz)">Alfonso und Estrella</a></i>, D.732
</dd><dd>b. from <i><a href="/wiki/Die_Zauberharfe,_D.644_(Schubert,_Franz)" title="Die Zauberharfe, D.644 (Schubert, Franz)">Die Zauberharfe</a></i>, D.644
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>1. Entr’acte nach dem 1. Aufzug
</dd><dd>2. Ballett
</dd><dd>3a. Entr’acte nach dem 2. Aufzug
</dd><dd>3b. Romanze. Der Vollmond strahlt auf Bergeshöh’n
</dd><dd>4. Geisterchor. In der Tiefe wohnt das Licht
</dd><dd>5. Entr’acte nach dem 3. Aufzug (Andantino in B-flat major)
</dd><dd>6. Hirtenmelodien
</dd><dd>7. Hirtenchor. Hier auf den Fluren
</dd><dd>8. Jägerchor. Wie lebt sich’s so fröhlich im Grünen
</dd><dd>9. Ballett
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1823
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1891 (complete work)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Ch%C3%A9zy,_Helmina_von" title="Category:Chézy, Helmina von">Helmina von Chézy</a> (1783–1856)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> mezzo-soprano (in Romanze, no.3b), mixed chorus (male chorus in no.4, mixed chorus in nos.7 and 8)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons, 4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones, timpani, strings
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Related Works
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/4_Impromptus,_D.935_(Schubert,_Franz)" title="4 Impromptus, D.935 (Schubert, Franz)">4 Impromptus, D.935</a>: theme from <i>Rosamunde</i> used in No.3<br /><a href="/wiki/String_Quartet_No.13,_D.804_(Schubert,_Franz)" title="String Quartet No.13, D.804 (Schubert, Franz)">String Quartet No.13, D.804</a>: theme from <i>Rosamunde</i> used in the Andante<br /><a href="/wiki/Symphony_No.8,_D.759_(Schubert,_Franz)" title="Symphony No.8, D.759 (Schubert, Franz)">Symphony No.8, D.759</a>: Conjecturally, finale originally composed for this symphony ended up as 2nd (B minor) Entr'acte (No.5) to this incidental music.
</td></tr>
<tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Publication_History">Publication History</span></h4>
<ul><li>3b. Romanze,&#160;»Der Vollmond strahlt auf Bergeshöh’n«, published as Op.26 (1824).
</li><li>8., 4. and 7. as "Heft 2 - 4" of the previous, and 4. in parts (1828).
</li><li>1. and 5. as orchestral score (1866, according to Deutsch catalog, German edition).
</li><li>Overture "Die Zauberharfe", 1. and 5. (Entr'actes), 9. and 2 (Ballett music), in an orchestral collection (Vianna: C.A. Spina, 1867).
</li><li>3a and 6 in: "Alte Gesamtausgabe", complete work with the overture to "Alfonso und Estrella" (1891). 
</li></ul>
